#
# CyberRax's combined blocklist for additional advertisement and malware domains
# release 12  (250522)
# Free to use for non-commercial purposes
#
# - meant to be used on a router to protect the whole LAN, either via modern Tomato firmware with haarp's ADBlock.sh v4.5+ script
#   ( http://www.linksysinfo.org/index.php?threads/script-clean-lean-and-mean-adblocking.68464/ ) or jerrm's modification of it
#   ( http://www.linksysinfo.org/index.php?threads/script-adblock-not-so-lean.72290/ ), via the built-in adblocking option in case
#   of FreshTomato firmware, or through AsusWRT-Merlin firmware with Diversion ( https://diversion.ch/ ) or the older AB-Solution
#   ( http://ab-solution.info/).
#   Alternatively any HOSTS manager (a'la AdAway) can use this list as well.
# - should be used together with another general purpose anti-ad list like P. Lowe's: http://pgl.yoyo.org/adservers/
# - is updated irregularly, about 1-2x year
#
# Changelog:
#
#   r12 - phishing site mimicing Estonian Tax Agency
#         new malware addresses from Zimperium's blog
#   r11 - additional encountered domains
#         added domains used by RatMilad spyware and IRGC-affiliated actors
#         latest data from all lists
#   r10 - added domains used by Conti malware
#         latest data from all lists
#    r9 - added addresses used by FlyTrap, PhoneSpy and SharkBot malwares
#    r8 - added most domains used by the GiftHorse malware
#         latest data from all lists
#    r7 - added WaLLy3K's personal list (comments following domains is not well handled by my modified NotSoLean script)
#         added Disconnect.me's advertising list
#         removed Sudaraka's, Schnack's and abuse.ch's lists (discontinued)
#         latest data from all lists
#    r6 - re-added all Spam404 entries for blockers that only support HOSTS format and not domain lists
#         added Disconnect.me's malvertising blocklist
#         added abuse.ch's ransomware and ZeuS malware blocklists
#         latest data from all lists
#    r5 - follows HOSTS convention to actually work with non-modified ADBlock
#         removed DigitalThrottle's list, as it seems to have been discontinued (and contained false positives)
#         latest data from all the included lists
#    r4 - removed most Spam404 entries, as they have a separate downloadable list available now
#         separate sections for SpywareBlaster (from registry) and SpyBot (from HOSTS)
#         latest data from all the included lists
#    r3 - added malware domains added by SpywareBlaster and SpyBot to Win's registry
#         added the 15000+ domains Spybot puts into the HOSTS file
#
###############################################################################################
